USE [lwglobaltest]
GO
--drop table [dbo].[ltblPlayerMain]
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[ltblPlayerMain]
(
	[NameID] [int] NOT NULL,
	[UserName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[Name] [varchar](40) NOT NULL,
	[Surname] [varchar](40) NOT NULL,
	[PlayerCityID] [int] NOT NULL,
	[PlayerCountryID] [int] NOT NULL,
	[Capital] [float] NOT NULL default(0),
	[NetWorth] [float] NOT NULL default(0),
	[PlayerRankID] [int] NOT NULL default(0)
    CONSTRAINT PK_NameID PRIMARY KEY (NameID,UserName)
    CONSTRAINT FK_PlayerCity FOREIGN KEY (PlayerCityID) REFERENCES ltblCities(CityID)
)

GO

--------
--drop table [dbo].[ltblCities]
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[ltblCities]
(
	[CityID] [int] NOT NULL,
	[CityAscii] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
	[MaxSize] [float] NOT NULL,
	[LandAvail] [float] NOT NULL,
	[Pop] [float] NOT NULL,
	[Cost] [float] NOT NULL,
	[IsoCodeCountry] [varchar] (3) NOT NULL

	 CONSTRAINT PK_CityID PRIMARY KEY (CityID)
	--to tie up FK to CountryID after import
	-- CONSTRAINT FK_CountryID FOREIGN KEY (CountryID) REFERENCES ltblCountries(CountryID)
)

GO

--drop table [dbo].[ltblCountries]
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[ltblCountries]
(
	[CountryID] [int] NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1),
	[CountryISOCode] [varchar] (3) NOT NULL,
	[CountryName] [varchar](75) NOT NULL

	 CONSTRAINT PK_CountryID PRIMARY KEY (CountryID)
)

GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[ltblCommodities](
	[CommodityID] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[CommodityCode] [varchar](4) NOT NULL,
 	[CommodityDesc] [varchar](25) NOT NULL,
	[BaseCostUSD] [money] NOT NULL,
	[Quantity] [float] NOT NULL DEFAULT (0),
	[CanBeRefined] [int] NOT NULL,
	[IndustryType] [Int] NOT NULL,
	[Unit] [varchar](3) NOT NULL,
	[Country]  [varchar](3) NOT NULL,
	[ProcessTo] [int] NOT NULL
 CONSTRAINT [PK_CommodityID] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[CommodityID] ASC
))

GO
